msg:We traveled off-peak before the Dragon Boat Festival, and stayed at Jinling Yadu Hotel for the three-day and two-night Suzhou trip. The hotel has a very design-oriented exterior, and the foyer and lobby are very atmospheric and upscale. The parent-child room is very warmly decorated, with special children's toiletries and a small corner for games. The hotel is located in a non-restricted area, with a large parking lot, very friendly to self-driving, across the road is the subway station, and it is not far to take a taxi to the main attractions. The location is impeccable. The best thing is the super five-star service. Every beautiful morning starts in the breakfast room, and the service staff always welcomes warmly. Special thanks to Miss Honghua, knowing that I am traveling with the elderly, she specially prepared fruits and snacks for us to eat on the road, which is really thoughtful and considerate. The only minus point should be the TV, which feels a bit old, and the picture quality is not very good. Although young people rarely watch it, the elderly still need it.

msg:The room was booked as a family room, and I went there for the brand of Jinling Hotel. At first, I saw a big bed room and a small bed room. The view on the 22nd floor was pretty good, but the experience was very speechless. I won't book it again next time! It's said to be a five-star hotel, but it's not as good as a better three-star hotel. First of all, the mattress of the big bed is okay, but the small bed is completely unreliable and the mattress is very hard. I slept all night with back pain, and the most speechless thing is that there is no socket, no light switch, and no TV remote control at the head of the small bed, which is very inconvenient; secondly, the air conditioner is very old, and the sound of the air supply after turning it on makes it impossible to sleep, and it doesn't cool at all, which is very bad. I was sweating after taking a shower, and there was no ventilation system in the bathroom. The bathtub was even more mottled and looked very dirty! The toilet is also the most ordinary old-fashioned toilet! I called the service desk and they said that the cooling would not be turned on this day, and they repeatedly emphasized that no other guests reported that it was too hot, so they would not turn on the cooling for one room. Later, I asked back, if others don't report my problem, won't they solve it? The service desk reluctantly agreed to turn it on for an hour, but it was really speechless. The cooling effect of the air conditioner was too slow! I don't know if it was just a perfunctory response. I was too lazy to communicate with him later in the evening! I also booked the revolving restaurant on the 29th floor, which was 188 per person and 150 per person for hotel guests, but the price/performance ratio was too low. I can only say that only the 29th floor attracted me. The breakfast on the first floor was also average. The fruits were watermelon, banana and pear. The Su-style breakfast was just one fried dumpling. There was nothing special about the other items. It was not as good as the 40 per person at the Four Seasons Hotel. Bad review, bad review, bad review!!!

msg:The next day after arriving in Yangzhou, we had to arrange accommodation for the next stop, Suzhou, because we planned to take the high-speed rail from Yangzhou to Suzhou on Friday morning and check in at the hotel on Friday afternoon. Moreover, the hotel stay spanned the entire weekend (Saturday and Sunday), which was the peak period for hotel check-in. Not only was it difficult to find a hotel, but the price would definitely soar. Therefore, although we were very tired after a day of wandering around (Slender West Lake, Geyuan Garden, Yechun for dinner, and taking an electric tricycle to tour the alleys of Yangzhou), as soon as we entered the hotel room (Holiday Inn Express Yangzhou Slender West Lake Wenchang Pavilion), we still forced ourselves to log in to Ctrip to search for Suzhou hotels. After a multi-dimensional search, we finally found this five-star Suzhou Jinling Yadu Hotel in the hotel rankings. This hotel is very close to the old city wall of Daoqian Street. Although it is outside the traditional Gusu city, it still belongs to the Gusu District. It is very close to the Tiger Hill Scenic Area, Hanshan Temple, Maple Bridge Scenic Area, Xiyuan Temple, and Lingering Garden. It is also very convenient to go to the Humble Administrator's Garden, Lion Grove, Pingjiang Road, Guanqian Street and Qilishantang Scenic Area from the hotel. Not only that, even with all the weekend peaks included, the price is still within my comfort zone. So I quickly placed the order. When we checked in on Friday afternoon, Ms. Fang Fang, who greeted us at the hotel front desk, was warm and thoughtful, leaving us with a very good first impression. After entering the room, I was also satisfied with the overall facilities. Living on a high floor, the view is very wide and the surrounding scenery is in full view. The breakfast on the first floor of the hotel is not only rich in variety, but also tastes very good. It is particularly worth mentioning that bowl of small wontons, whether it is the size of the wontons, the thickness of the skin, the size, looseness and taste of the fillings, the deliciousness of the soup, and the moderate number of wontons in each bowl, are infinitely close to my pursuit and expectation of wontons. In short, the four days of staying at Suzhou Jinling Yadu Hotel will be a very good memory.
